msg:We drove to Hengdian by ourselves. The hotel is not far from the scenic spot and can be reached in 20 minutes. Parking at the hotel is also relatively convenient. When we walked into the lobby, we were shocked by the splendid decoration. The wood carvings and mahogany home furnishings more than ten meters high highlight the beauty of the hotel. The hotel has a high-end a**osphere, and the room you stay in is also very clean and hygienic, with complete facilities. There are rich dishes for breakfast and dinner, and a buffet seafood meal for dinner, which is very cost-effective. The outdoor swimming pool was not open in April. Considering that the children wanted to play in the water, we asked the lady at the front desk if we could arrange a room with a bathtub. Unexpectedly, the front desk quickly arranged for us to change rooms for free. Thank you very much to Xiao Qiao and Xiao Qin. The warm service and small gifts provided by the front desk made our children very happy to play in the water. The last thing I want to add is that free fruit was given when checking in. The service is thoughtful and considerate. I will book this hotel next time.
